INNER JOIN "Customers" AS c ON o."CustomerId" = c."Id"
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT o0."Id", o0."UserId", u."FullName", o0."Cost", o0."WorkerRole", o0."AssignedAt", o0."OrderId"
    FROM "OrderWorkers" AS o0
    INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON o0."UserId" = u."Id"
) AS t ON o."Id" = t."OrderId"
ORDER BY o."Id" DESC, c."Id"
